<script>
    
    $(function() {

        var offsetNext = '21';
        var offsetPrev = '-19';
        var queryStr = '&amp;sortby&#x3D;sortByDateDesc&amp;imprintname&#x3D;Academic Press';
        var tmpStr = '';
        
        if(offsetPrev >= 1) { // Has prev (>= 1 workaround for the -19 offset)
            tmpStr += '<link rel="prev" href="/catalog?start_rank='+ offsetPrev + queryStr + '" />';
        }

        if(offsetNext) { // Has next
            tmpStr += '<link rel="next" href="/catalog?start_rank='+ offsetNext + queryStr + '" />';
        }

        $('head').append(tmpStr);

    });

</script>

  var categoriesLevel1 = null;
  var categoriesLevel2 = null;
  var categoriesLevel3 = null;

  for (var i = 0; i < categoriesLevel0.length; i++) {
      var currentOptionGroup = $('<optgroup/>').attr('label', categoriesLevel0[i].Name);
      $('#categories-level-0').append(currentOptionGroup);

      categoriesLevel1 = categoriesLevel0[i].Children;
      if (!categoriesLevel1) {
          continue;
      }

      for (var j = 0; j < categoriesLevel1.length; j++) {
          currentOptionGroup.append(
              $('<option/>')
                .attr('value', categoriesLevel1[j].Slug)
                .text(categoriesLevel1[j].Name)
          );

          if (categoriesLevel1[j].ID == viewableCategoryChain[0].id) {
              categoriesLevel2 = categoriesLevel1[j].Children;
          }
      }
  }

  if (viewableCategoryChain[0].slug) {
      $('#categories-level-0')
          .find('option[value="' + viewableCategoryChain[0].slug + '"]')
          .attr('selected', true);

      if (categoriesLevel2) {
        $('.categories-level-2').append(
            $('<option value=""/>').text('All Subject Areas')
        );

        for(var i = 0; i < categoriesLevel2.length; i++) {
            $('.categories-level-2').append(
                $('<option/>')
                  .attr('value', categoriesLevel2[i].Slug)
                  .text(categoriesLevel2[i].Name)
            );

            if (categoriesLevel2[i].ID == viewableCategoryChain[1].id) {
                categoriesLevel3 = categoriesLevel2[i].Children;
            }
        }
      }
  }

  if (viewableCategoryChain[1].slug) {
      $('.categories-level-2')
          .find('option[value="' + viewableCategoryChain[1].slug + '"]')
          .attr('selected', true);

      if (categoriesLevel3) {
        $('.categories-level-3').append(
            $('<option value=""/>').text('All Subject Areas')
        );

        for(var i = 0; i < categoriesLevel3.length; i++) {
            $('.categories-level-3').append(
                $('<option/>')
                  .attr('value', categoriesLevel3[i].Slug)
                  .text(categoriesLevel3[i].Name)
            );
        }
      }
  }

  if (viewableCategoryChain[2].slug) {
      $('.categories-level-3')
          .find('option[value="' + viewableCategoryChain[2].slug + '"]')
          .attr('selected', true);
  }


  $('[class*=categories-level-]').attr('disabled', false);
  $('[class*=categories-level-]:empty').html("<option value=''>Related Subject Areas</option>").attr('disabled', true);

  $('#categories-level-0').on('change', function() {
      $('.categories-level-2').val("");
      $('.categories-level-3').val("");
      submitForm();
  });

  $('[class*=categories-level-2]').on('change', function() {
      $('.categories-level-3').val("");
      submitForm();
  });

  $('[class*=categories-level-3]').on('change', function() {
      submitForm();
  });

  var urlPrettifier = (function () {
      function buildPrettyCategoryUrl(changeOrigin) {
          var urlParameters = [];

          if($('#categories-level-0 option:selected').val() !== '0') {
              urlParameters.push('cat0=' + $('#categories-level-0 option:selected').val());
          }

          if(($('#categories-level-2 option:selected').val()) &&
             ($('#categories-level-2 option:selected').val() !== '0') &&
             (changeOrigin !== 'cat0')) {
              urlParameters.push('cat1=' + $('#categories-level-2 option:selected').val());
          }

          if(($('#categories-level-3 option:selected').val()) &&
             ($('#categories-level-3 option:selected').val() !== '0') &&
             ($('#categories-level-3 option:selected').val() !== 'Related Subject Areas') &&
             (changeOrigin !== 'cat0') &&
             (changeOrigin !== 'cat1'))  {
              urlParameters.push('cat2=' + $('#categories-level-3 option:selected').val());
          }

          // do string concat at the end. More efficient as you're not creating a load of strings.
          return urlParameters.join('&');
      }

      return { buildPrettyCategoryUrl: buildPrettyCategoryUrl };
  })();
</script>
<script>
  function generateRedirect(newUrl) {
    if (newUrl === '') {
      newUrl = window.location.href.split("?")[0];
    }
    window.location = newUrl;
  }

  function defaultPaginate(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      var newUrl = buildUrl('other');
      var href = $(this).attr('href');
      if (newUrl.indexOf('?') === -1) {
          newUrl += href;
      } else {
          href = href.substring(1);
          newUrl += '&' + href;
      }
      generateRedirect(newUrl);
      return false;
  }

  function defaultClearFilter(e) {
      e.preventDefault();
      generateRedirect('');
      return false;
  }
</script>

    if (isMobile()) { // for mobile use native multiselect instead
        $filters_years.attr("multiple", "multiple");
        $filters_years.prepend("<option value=''>All publication years</option>");
        $filters_years.prepend("<optgroup disabled hidden></optgroup>"); // this solves iphone bug where it keeps choosing first option
        if (yearFilter) {
            $filters_years.val(yearFilter.split(","));
        } else {
            $filters_years.val("");
        }

        $filters_years.on('blur', function() {
            submitForm();
       });
    } else {
        $(function () {
            $filters_years.attr("multiple", "multiple");
            $filters_years.multipleSelect({
                filter: true,
                allSelected: "All Publication Years",
                onCheckAll: function () {
                    checkedAll = true;
                },
                onUncheckAll: function () {
                    checkedAll = false;
                },
                onClick: function() {
                    yearsChanged = true;
                },
                onClose: function() {
                    if (yearsChanged) {
                        submitForm();
                    }
                },
                onTypingInFilter: function (input) {
                    if(input) {
                        yearSearchFilterUsed = true;
                    } else {
                        yearSearchFilterUsed = false;
                    }
                }
            });
            if (yearFilter) {
                $filters_years.multipleSelect('setSelects', yearFilter.split(","));
            } else {
                $filters_years.multipleSelect('uncheckAll');
            }
        });
    }

  //Reset filters after post back.
  if (productTypeFilter) {
      $('#filters_type').val(productTypeFilter);
  }

  if (queryFilter) {
      $filters_query.val(queryFilter);
  }

  if (sortBy) {
      $('#filters_sortBy').val(sortBy);
  }

  $('#filters_type, #filters_sortBy').on('change', function() {
      submitForm();
  });

  $('#search_authors').click(function() {
      submitForm();
  });

// to trigger search query when pressing enter
  $filters_query.keypress(function( event ) {
      if ( event.which == 13 ) {
        submitForm();
      }
  });

// only use suggestion for non-mobile, cause suggestion list covers the seach button in mobile view
if (!isMobile()) {
    $filters_query.autocomplete({
    minLength: 2,
    source: function(request, response) {
        var results = $.ui.autocomplete.filter(availableAuthors, request.term);
        response(results.slice(0, 20));
    },
    select: function( event, ui ) {
        $filters_query.val("");
        $('#filters_authors').val(ui.item.value);
        submitForm();
    }
    });
}

// to set to all option if it is chosen and clear the rest, no need to send all dates chosen if all is selected
function submitForm() {

    /**
     * if a user is searching for author, we want to default sorting to releveance, however if the user decides to change the sort-by we keep it
     * this is done by checking if the author was entered fot the first time, then default to relevence, but if author name is the same as previuos submit, but the sortby has changed
     * it means the user wants a different sort-by so dont change it
     */
    if ($filters_query.val() && queryFilter != $filters_query.val()) {
        $('#filters_sortBy').val("sortByRelevance");
    }

    if (isMobile()) { // in mobile view if a user chooses particular years along side the all-years being still checked, then i
        if($.isArray($filters_years.val())) {
            if ($.inArray("", $filters_years.val()) > -1) {
                var yearsArray = $filters_years.val();
                for (var i = 0; i < yearsArray.length; i++) {
                    if (!yearsArray[i]) {
                        yearsArray.splice(i,1);
                        i--;
                    }
                }
                $filters_years.val(yearsArray);
            }
        }
    } else {
        if (checkedAll && !yearSearchFilterUsed) { // only send all years when filter is not being used, cause if list is filtered then only send the chosen years
            $filters_years.val("");
        }
    }
    $('#catalog-search-form').submit();
}

function isMobile() {
    if ( 
    !/iP(od|hone)/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !/IEMobile/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && 
    !/Windows Phone/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !/BlackBerry/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && 
    !/BB10/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent) && !/Android.*Mobile/i.test(window.navigator.userAgent)
    ) {
        return false;
    } else {
        return true;
    }
}

  $(function () {
      $('.purchase-subscriptions-link').click(function (event) {
          event.preventDefault();
          var elementWidth = $(this).outerWidth();
          $(this).next().css('width', elementWidth).toggle();
      });

      $(window).click(function (event) {
          if (!event.target.matches('.purchase-subscriptions-link')) {
              $('.dropdown-content').hide();
          }
      });
  });


</script>

<script  src="https://cdn.elsevier.io/matrix/ui/1.6.41/vendor.js"></script>
<script  src="https://cdn.elsevier.io/matrix/ui/1.6.41/scripts-bottom.js"></script>
<script>
var menuEvents = ['menu-home', 'menu-about', 'menu-careers', 'menu-connect', 'menu-authors', 'menu-editors', 'menu-librarians', 'menu-reviewers', 'menu-books-journals', 'menu-author-webshop', 'menu-rnd-solutions', 'menu-research-intelligence', 'menu-clinical-solution', 'menu-educational-solutions', 'menu-research-platform', 'menu-all-solutions'];
window['optimizely'] = window['optimizely'] || [];

$(function(){
  $.each(menuEvents, function(i,val){
    $(".menu-category-item:eq("+i+") a").on("click", function(e){
      window.optimizely.push(["trackEvent", menuEvents[i]]);
    });
  })

  $(".menu-external-link a").on("click", function(){
    window.optimizely.push(["trackEvent", "menu-support-center" ]);
  });
      
  $(".js-header-menu-toggle-open, .js-close-primary-menu").on("click", function(){
    window.optimizely.push(["trackEvent", "menu-clicked" ]);
  });
});
</script>

<div id="surveyPopup" class="survey-trigger" style="display:none;">
<script>
   surveyOptions = {
      startDate: 1380622914,
      endDate: 1609373814,
      frequency: '',
      url: 'https://survey.confirmit.com/wix2/p2683244022.aspx',
      inactive: 'No',
      target: 0.1,
      cookieName: 'survey'
  }
  // Increase frequency of survey to 1 in 100 visitors
  
    var urls = ["/journals/", "/books/", "/solutions/sciencedirect/content/articlechoice", "/solutions/embase-biomedical-research", "/solutions/geofacets"];
    
    var currentPath = window.location.pathname;
    
    urls = urls.filter(function(url) {
      return currentPath.indexOf(url)==0;
    });
    
    if(urls.length > 0) {
        surveyOptions.target = 1;  
    }
    
    $(function(){
      surveyInit(surveyOptions);
    })
</script>
